  </header> 
  <script>
  var $menu = $(".nav__dropdown_menu-item"),
      $right_menu = $(".right_dropdown-item"),
      is_mobile = checkDevice();

  if (!is_mobile) {
    // jQuery-menu-aim:
    // Hook up events to be fired on menu row activation.
    $menu.menuAim({
      rowSelector: '> div',
      activate: activateSubmenu,
      deactivate: deactivateSubmenu
    });

    $right_menu.menuAim({
      rowSelector: '> div',
      submenuDirection: 'left',
      activate: activateSubmenu,
      deactivate: deactivateSubmenu
    });

    $('.nav__dropdown__menu').mouseleave(function () {
      var $row = $('a.maintainHover').parent();

      deactivateSubmenu($row);
    });

    var timer;

    $(".nav_below_divider").mouseenter(function() {
      var $row = $('a.maintainHover').parent();
      timer = setTimeout(function() {
        deactivateSubmenu($row);
      }, 500);
    }).mouseleave(function() {
      clearTimeout(timer);
    });
  }
</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
  function toggleVisibility(element_id) {
    $('#'+element_id).toggle();
  }
  function toggleDivVisibility(prefix) {
    var element_id = prefix+'_full';
    var icon = prefix+'_icon';
    var state = document.getElementById(element_id).style;
    if (!$('#' + prefix + '_full').is(':visible')) {
      $('#' + prefix + '_icon').attr('src', 'https://sslcdn.proz.com/images/pftv6/icon_contract.gif');
      if (prefix =='standard') {
        $("#standard_text").html('Hide standardized information');
        $('#' + prefix + '_full').show();
      } else {
        $('#' + prefix + '_full_more').trigger('click');
      }
    }
    else {
      $('#' + prefix + '_icon').attr('src', 'https://sslcdn.proz.com/images/pftv6/icon_expand.gif');
      if (prefix =='standard') {
        $("#standard_text").html('Display standardized information');
        $('#' + prefix + '_full').hide();
      } else {
        $('#' + prefix + '_full_less').trigger('click');
      }
    }
  }
  
  function toggleTabClass(old_tab_id, new_tab_id) {
    var old_tab=document.getElementById(old_tab_id);
    var old_tab_url=document.getElementById(old_tab_id+'_url');
    var new_tab=document.getElementById(new_tab_id);
    var new_tab_url=document.getElementById(new_tab_id+'_url');
    old_tab.className='innertaboff';
    old_tab_url.className='innertaboff';
    new_tab.className='innertabon';
    new_tab_url.className='innertabon';
    ajax_cur_tab=new_tab_id;
  }
  
  function toggleDataClassInline(name) {
    var el = document.getElementById(name);
    var class_name = el.className;
    if (class_name=="pageText") {
      el.className = "hidden";
      if (name=='wwa') el.style.backgroundColor='#dddddd';
    }
    else {
     el.className = "pageText";
     if (name=='wwa') el.style.backgroundColor='#EFECD1';
    }
  }
  </script> 
  <script type="text/javascript">
  $(document).ready(function() {
    $(".more_link").click(function() {
      var id_str = $(this).attr('id');
      id_str = id_str.replace('_full_more', '');
      $('#' + id_str + '_icon').attr('src', 'https://sslcdn.proz.com/images/pftv6/icon_contract.gif');
    });
    $(".less_link").click(function() {
      var id_str = $(this).attr('id');
      id_str = id_str.replace('_full_less', '');
      $('#' + id_str + '_icon').attr('src', 'https://sslcdn.proz.com/images/pftv6/icon_expand.gif');
    });
  });
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
              var map;
              var markersArray = [];
              function loadMap() {
                var location = new google.maps.LatLng(34.1736, -118.603);
                var mapOptions = {
                  zoom: 4,
                  center: location,
                  disableDefaultUI: true,
                  zoomControl: true,
                  mapTypeControl: false,
                  scaleControl: false,
                  mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP
                };
                var image = new google.maps.MarkerImage("https://sslcdn.proz.com/images/mm_20_blue.png",
                  // This marker is 20 pixels wide by 32 pixels tall.
                  new google.maps.Size(12, 20),
                  // The origin for this image is 0,0.
                  new google.maps.Point(0,0),
                  // The anchor for this image is the base of the flagpole at 12,20.
                  new google.maps.Point(12,20)
                );
                map =  new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById("map"), mapOptions);
                marker = new google.maps.Marker({
                  position: location,
                  map: map,
                  icon: image,
                  shadow: "https://sslcdn.proz.com/images/mm_20_shadow.png"
                });
              }
              $(document).ready(function() {loadMap();});
            </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function() {
      $("#btn-more-actions").on("click", function(e) {
        $("#more-actions-dropdown").toggle();
        if ($("#more-actions-dropdown").is(":visible")) {
          $(this).find(".btn-caret").removeClass("fa-caret-down").addClass("fa-caret-up");
        } else {
          $(this).find(".btn-caret").removeClass("fa-caret-up").addClass("fa-caret-down");
        }
      });
    });
    </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
                var $footer = $("#footer_2017"),
                    current_margin = 0;
                $(document).ready(function() {
                   $(window).resize(correctFooterWidth($footer));
                    //correctFooterWidth();
                });

                function correctFooterWidth(footer) {
                    var correct_width = current_margin + $(window).width() - footer.width();
                    current_margin = correct_width;
                  $footer.css("margin-right", "-" + correct_width + "px");
                }
              </script>
